    <h2 id="introduction" style="margin:10px 0px; font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-weight:300; line-height:40px; color:rgb(136,136,136); font-size:26px; padding-top:50px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
     AndroidDevTools简介
    </h2>
    <blockquote style="padding:0px 0px 0px 15px; margin:0px 0px 20px; border-left-width:5px; border-left-style:solid; border-left-color:rgb(238,238,238); color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:17.5px; line-height:1.25">
      <strong>
       Android Dev Tools官网地址：
       <a href="http://www.androiddevtools.cn/" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="color:rgb(0,136,204); text-decoration:none" target="_blank">
        www.androiddevtools.cn
       </a>
      </strong>
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:17.5px; line-height:1.25">
      收集整理Android开发所需的Android SDK、开发中用到的工具、Android开发教程、Android设计规范，免费的设计素材等。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:17.5px; line-height:1.25">
      欢迎大家推荐自己在Android开发过程中用的好用的工具、学习开发教程、用到设计素材，欢迎Star、Fork 。
     </p>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:17.5px; line-height:1.25">
      如果你对翻译英文的Android开发技术文章感兴趣，欢迎Start和Fork
      <a href="https://github.com/AWCNTT/ArticleTranslateProject" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="color:rgb(0,136,204); text-decoration:none" target="_blank">
       AndroidWeekly中国文章翻译项目
      </a>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h2 id="android-dev-tools" style="margin:10px 0px; font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-weight:300; line-height:40px; color:rgb(136,136,136); font-size:26px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
     <a class="anchor" href="http://www.androiddevtools.cn/#android-tools" name="android-tools" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="color:rgb(0,136,204); text-decoration:none" target="_blank">
      <span class="octicon octicon-link">
      </span>
     </a>
     Android Tools
    </h2>
    <h5 style="margin:10px 0px; font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-weight:400; line-height:20px; color:rgb(136,136,136); font-size:18px; padding-top:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
     <a class="anchor" href="http://www.androiddevtools.cn/#android-sdk%E5%9C%A8%E7%BA%BF%E6%9B%B4%E6%96%B0%E9%95%9C%E5%83%8F%E6%9C%8D%E5%8A%A1%E5%99%A8" id="android-sdk-online-server" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="color:rgb(0,136,204); text-decoration:none" target="_blank">
      <span class="octicon octicon-link">
      </span>
     </a>
     Android SDK在线更新镜像服务器
    </h5>
    <ol style="padding:0px; margin:0px 0px 10px 25px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
     <li>
      <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px">
       中国科学院开源协会镜像站地址:
      </p>
      <ul style="padding:0px; margin:0px 0px 0px 25px">
       <li>
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px">
         IPV4/IPV6:
         <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
          http://mirrors.opencas.cn
         </code>
         端口：80
        </p>
       </li>
       <li>
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px">
         IPV4/IPV6:
         <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
          http://mirrors.opencas.org
         </code>
         端口：80
        </p>
       </li>
       <li>
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px">
         IPV4/IPV6:
         <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
          http://mirrors.opencas.ac.cn
         </code>
         端口：80
        </p>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px">
       上海GDG镜像服务器地址:
      </p>
      <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px">
       <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
        http://sdk.gdgshanghai.com
       </code>
       端口：8000
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px">
       北京化工大学镜像服务器地址:
      </p>
      <ul style="padding:0px; margin:0px 0px 0px 25px">
       <li>
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px">
         IPv4:
         <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
          http://ubuntu.buct.edu.cn/
         </code>
         端口：80
        </p>
       </li>
       <li>
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px">
         IPv4:
         <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
          http://ubuntu.buct.cn/
         </code>
         端口：80
        </p>
       </li>
       <li>
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px">
         IPv6:
         <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
          http://ubuntu.buct6.edu.cn/
         </code>
         端口：80
        </p>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px">
       大连东软信息学院镜像服务器地址:
      </p>
      <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px">
       <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
        http://mirrors.neusoft.edu.cn
       </code>
       端口：80
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
     <strong>
      使用方法
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ol style="padding:0px; margin:0px 0px 10px 25px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
     <li>
      <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px">
       启动 Android SDK Manager ，打开主界面，依次选择『
       <strong>
        Tools
       </strong>
       』、『
       <strong>
        Options...
       </strong>
       』，弹出『
       <strong>
        Android SDK Manager - Settings
       </strong>
       』窗口；
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px">
       在『
       <strong>
        Android SDK Manager - Settings
       </strong>
       』窗口中，在『
       <strong>
        HTTP Proxy Server」和「HTTP Proxy Port
       </strong>
       』输入框内填入上面镜像服务器地址(
       <strong>
        不包含http://
       </strong>
       ，如下图)和端口，并且选中『
       <strong>
        Force https://... sources to be fetched using http://...
       </strong>
       』复选框。设置完成后单击『
       <strong>
        Close
       </strong>
       』按钮关闭『
       <strong>
        Android SDK Manager - Settings
       </strong>
       』窗口返回到主界面；
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px">
       依次选择『
       <strong>
        Packages
       </strong>
       』、『
       <strong>
        Reload
       </strong>
       』。
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>

     <blockquote style="padding:0px 0px 0px 15px; margin:0px 0px 20px; border-left-width:5px; border-left-style:solid; border-left-color:rgb(238,238,238); color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; font-size:17.5px; line-height:1.25">
       <strong>
        备注：
       </strong>
       <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
        非官方版
       </code>
       是在
       <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
        23.0.2
       </code>
       的基础上进行了在线更新包含了
       <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
        Android 5.0 SDK
       </code>
       ，
       <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
        SDK Tools 23.0.5
       </code>
       、
       <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
        Build Tools 21.0.1
       </code>
       、
       <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
        Support Library 21
       </code>
       等。
      </p>
     </blockquote>
     <h5 style="margin:10px 0px; font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-weight:400; line-height:20px; color:rgb(136,136,136); font-size:18px; padding-top:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      <a class="anchor" href="http://www.androiddevtools.cn/#sdk-platform-tools" id="sdk-platform-tools" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="color:rgb(0,136,204); text-decoration:none" target="_blank">
       <span class="octicon octicon-link">
       </span>
      </a>
      SDK Platform-Tools
     </h5>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      这是 adb, fastboot 等工具包。把解压出来的
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       platform-tools
      </code>
      文件夹放在 android sdk 根目录下，并把
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       adb
      </code>
      所在的目录添加到系统
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       PATH
      </code>
      路径里，即可在命令行里直接访问了 adb, fastboot 等工具。
     </p>
     <table style="max-width:100%; background-color:rgb(246,246,246); border-collapse:collapse; border-spacing:0px; border:1px solid rgb(177,177,177); margin-bottom:20px; text-align:center; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px">

      <a class="anchor" href="http://www.androiddevtools.cn/#build-tools" id="build-tools" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="color:rgb(0,136,204); text-decoration:none" target="_blank">

     </h5>

      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       your sdk 路径/build-tools
      </code>
      文件夹即可。
     </p>

     <h5 id="sdk-list" style="margin:10px 0px; font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-weight:400; line-height:20px; color:rgb(136,136,136); font-size:18px; padding-top:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      <a class="anchor" href="http://www.androiddevtools.cn/#sdk-list" name="sdk" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="color:rgb(0,136,204); text-decoration:none" target="_blank">
       <span class="octicon octicon-link">
       </span>
      </a>
      SDK
     </h5>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      这是Android开发所需的sdk，下载并解压后，将解压出的整个文件夹复制或者移动到
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       your sdk 路径/platforms
      </code>
      文件夹，然后打开SDK Manager，打开
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Tools(工具)
      </code>
      菜单选择
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Options(选项)
      </code>
      菜单项打开Android SDK Manager Setting对话框，点击
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Clear Cache(清除缓存)
      </code>
      按钮，然后重启Eclipse(或Android Studio)和SDK Manager。
     </p>

     <h5 id="sdk-system-images" style="margin:10px 0px; font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-weight:400; line-height:20px; color:rgb(136,136,136); font-size:18px; padding-top:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      <a class="anchor" href="http://www.androiddevtools.cn/#sdk-system-images" name="sdk-system-images" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="color:rgb(0,136,204); text-decoration:none" target="_blank">
       <span class="octicon octicon-link">
       </span>
      </a>
      SDK System images
     </h5>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      这是在创建模拟器时需要的system image，也就是在创建模拟器时
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       CPU/ABI
      </code>
      项需要选择的，下载并解压后，将解压出的整个文件夹复制或者移动到
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       your sdk 路径/system-images
      </code>
      文件夹下即可， 如果没有
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       system-images
      </code>
      目录就先创建此文件夹，然后打开SDK Manager，打开
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Tools(工具)
      </code>
      菜单选择
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Options(选项)
      </code>
      菜单项打开Android SDK Manager Setting对话框，点击
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Clear Cache(清除缓存)
      </code>
      按钮，然后重启Eclipse(或Android Studio)和SDK Manager。
     </p>

     <h5 id="googlemap-apis-sdk" style="margin:10px 0px; font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-weight:400; line-height:20px; color:rgb(136,136,136); font-size:18px; padding-top:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      <a class="anchor" href="http://www.androiddevtools.cn/#googlemap-apis-sdk" name="googlemap-apis-sdk" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="color:rgb(0,136,204); text-decoration:none" target="_blank">
       <span class="octicon octicon-link">
       </span>
      </a>
      GoogleMap APIs SDK
     </h5>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      这是GoogleMap APIs SDK，下载并解压后，将解压出的整个文件夹复制或者移动到
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       your sdk 路径/add-ons
      </code>
      文件夹下，然后打开SDK Manager，打开
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Tools(工具)
      </code>
      菜单选择
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Options(选项)
      </code>
      菜单项打开Android SDK Manager Setting对话框，点击
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Clear Cache(清除缓存)
      </code>
      按钮，然后重启Eclipse(或Android Studio)和SDK Manager。
     </p>

     <h5 id="google-glass-sdk" style="margin:10px 0px; font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-weight:400; line-height:20px; color:rgb(136,136,136); font-size:18px; padding-top:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      <a class="anchor" href="http://www.androiddevtools.cn/#google-glass-sdk" name="google-glass-sdk" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="color:rgb(0,136,204); text-decoration:none" target="_blank">
       <span class="octicon octicon-link">
       </span>
      </a>
      Google Glass SDK
     </h5>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      这是GDK，下载并解压后，将解压出的整个文件夹复制或者移动到
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       your sdk 路径/add-ons
      </code>
      文件夹下，然后打开SDK Manager，打开
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Tools(工具)
      </code>
      菜单选择
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Options(选项)
      </code>
      菜单项打开Android SDK Manager Setting对话框，点击
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Clear Cache(清除缓存)
      </code>
      按钮，然后重启Eclipse(或Android Studio)和SDK Manager。
     </p>
     <table style="max-width:100%; background-color:rgb(246,246,246); border-collapse:collapse; border-spacing:0px; border:1px solid rgb(177,177,177); margin-bottom:20px; text-align:center; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px">

     <h5 id="android-framework-source-code" style="margin:10px 0px; font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-weight:400; line-height:20px; color:rgb(136,136,136); font-size:18px; padding-top:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      <a class="anchor" href="http://www.androiddevtools.cn/#android-framework-source-code" name="android-framework-source-code" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="color:rgb(0,136,204); text-decoration:none" target="_blank">
       <span class="octicon octicon-link">
       </span>
      </a>
      Android Framework Source Code
     </h5>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      这是Android Framework Source Code，下载并解压后，将解压出的整个文件夹复制或者移动到
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       your sdk 路径/sources
      </code>
      文件夹下，然后重启Eclipse(或Android Studio)，这样当你在Eclipse里面按住
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Ctrl
      </code>
      键点击某个系统类时就可以打开该类的源码文件查看源码了。
     </p>

     <h5 id="android-sdk-extras" style="margin:10px 0px; font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-weight:400; line-height:20px; color:rgb(136,136,136); font-size:18px; padding-top:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      <a class="anchor" href="http://www.androiddevtools.cn/#android-sdk-extras" name="android-sdk-extras" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="color:rgb(0,136,204); text-decoration:none" target="_blank">
       <span class="octicon octicon-link">
       </span>
      </a>
      Android SDK Extras
     </h5>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      包含
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Android Support Library
      </code>
      、
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Google Cloud Messaging for Android Library
      </code>
      、
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Google Play services
      </code>
      、
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Google Play services for fit preview
      </code>
      、
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Google Play services for Froyo
      </code>
      、
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Google Play APK Expansion Library
      </code>
      、
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Google Play Billing Library
      </code>
      、
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Google Play Licensing Library
      </code>
      等，下载解压后将解压出的整个文件夹复制或者移动到
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       your sdk
      </code>
      根目录下下，如果已经存在
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       extras
      </code>
      文件夹就替换掉。
     </p>

     <h5 id="support-library" style="margin:10px 0px; font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-weight:400; line-height:20px; color:rgb(136,136,136); font-size:18px; padding-top:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      <a class="anchor" href="http://www.androiddevtools.cn/#support-library" name="support-library" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="color:rgb(0,136,204); text-decoration:none" target="_blank">
       <span class="octicon octicon-link">
       </span>
      </a>
      Support Library
     </h5>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      包含supportive、v7和v13，下载解压后将解压出的整个文件夹复制或者移动到
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       your sdk 路径/extras
      </code>
      下，然后打开SDK Manager，打开
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Tools(工具)
      </code>
      菜单选择
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Options(选项)
      </code>
      菜单项打开Android SDK Manager Setting对话框，点击
      <code style="padding:2px 4px; font-family:Monaco,Menlo,Consolas,'Courier New',monospace; font-size:12px; color:rgb(102,102,102); white-space:nowrap; background-color:transparent; border:0px">
       Clear Cache(清除缓存)
      </code>
      按钮，然后重启Eclipse(或Android Studio)和SDK Manager。
     </p>
     <table style="max-width:100%; background-color:rgb(246,246,246); border-collapse:collapse; border-spacing:0px; border:1px solid rgb(177,177,177); margin-bottom:20px; text-align:center; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px">

        </th>

     <h5 id="adt-bundle" style="margin:10px 0px; font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-weight:400; line-height:20px; color:rgb(136,136,136); font-size:18px; padding-top:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      <a class="anchor" href="http://www.androiddevtools.cn/#adt-bundle" name="adt-bundle" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="color:rgb(0,136,204); text-decoration:none" target="_blank">
       <span class="octicon octicon-link">
       </span>
      </a>
      ADT Bundle
     </h5>
     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      ADT Bundle包含了Eclipse、ADT插件和SDK Tools，是已经集成好的IDE，只需安装好Jdk即可开始开发，推荐初学者下载ADT Bundle，不用再折腾开发环境。
     </p>

         <br/>
         环境，让测试工程师们能够快速对智能手机和App在
         <br/>
         不同国家地区和应用环境下的性能表现进行测试。
        </td>
        <td align="center" style="padding:10px; border:1px solid rgb(177,177,177)">
         <a href="https://github.com/facebook/augmented-traffic-control" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="color:rgb(0,136,204); text-decoration:none" target="_blank">
          下载
         </a>
        </td>
        <td align="center" style="padding:10px; border:1px solid rgb(177,177,177)">
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>

     <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:10px; color:rgb(51,51,51); font-family:Roboto,sans-serif; font-size:15px; line-height:20px; background-color:rgb(246,246,246)">
      出自：
      <a href="http://stackoverflow.com/questions/5445085/understanding-colors-in-android-6-chars" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" style="color:rgb(0,136,204); text-decoration:none" target="_blank">

      </a>
